\hypertarget{interface_thing_smart_device}{}\doxysection{Thing\+Smart\+Device Class Reference}
\label{interface_thing_smart_device}\index{ThingSmartDevice@{ThingSmartDevice}}


The basic operation class of \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_device}{Thing\+Smart\+Device}} contains the model of basic information, including the device, DPs to send, update device information, and other common API operations.  




{\ttfamily \#import $<$Thing\+Smart\+Device.\+h$>$}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The basic operation class of \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_device}{Thing\+Smart\+Device}} contains the model of basic information, including the device, DPs to send, update device information, and other common API operations. 

All types of devices can be controlled after you initialize an instance of this class if the function is supported. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{ios-arm64__x86__64-simulator_2_thing_smart_device_core_kit_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_smart_device_8h_source_l00196}{196}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{ios-arm64__x86__64-simulator_2_thing_smart_device_core_kit_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_smart_device_8h_source}{Thing\+Smart\+Device.\+h}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily -\/ (void) send\+Cache\+Dps\+: \begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(NSDictionary $\ast$)}]{dps }\item[{validity\+:(NSUInteger)}]{validity }\item[{dp\+Cache\+Type\+:(NSUInteger)}]{dp\+Cache\+Type }\item[{success\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{watchos-arm64__arm64__32__armv7k_2_thing_smart_util_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_smart_util_8h_a1ac4228c704d9d5a24b47a8d3b9d4c32}{Thing\+Success\+ID}})}]{success }\item[{failure\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_af2b46bef0575729ec6391704cfc8a038}{Thing\+Failure\+Error}})}]{failure }\end{DoxyParamCaption}}

Publish dps cached in the cloud, and then the device itself requests to pull OR receives push from cloud.

{\bfseries{Note\+: Only suitable for low-\/power device.}} When the device is dormant, sending dps through this API will be cached in the cloud for a period of time. When the device wakes up within the validity period, the device can get the cached {\ttfamily dps}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dps} & The DP dictionary. \\
\hline
{\em validity} & The cached dps validity period. (Unit\+: second, Range\+: 1 $\sim$ 172800). \\
\hline
{\em dp\+Cache\+Type} & The dps cache type. ( {\ttfamily 0}\+: device itself requests to pull, {\ttfamily 1}\+: device receives push from cloud). \\
\hline
{\em success} & Called when the task is finished. \\
\hline
{\em failure} & Called when the task is interrupted by an error. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
